59</a></li></ul></li></ul></div></details></div><div class="center-images stack stack--block type"><div class="aside aside--note"><p>Interested in helping improve DevTools? Sign up to participate in <a href="https://google.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_9YbKj35IGoGsDBj?reserved=1&amp;utm_source=Website%20feature&amp;Q_Language=en&amp;utm_medium=own_web&amp;utm_campaign=Q4&amp;productTag=chrm&amp;campaignDate=November2020&amp;referral_code=UXFm430458">Google User Research here</a>.</p></div><div class="youtube"><lite-youtube videoid="-dOYxJnRhxQ" title="Play: Video"> </lite-youtube></div><h2 id="css" tabindex="-1"><a href="#css" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> New section for custom properties in Elements &gt; Styles</h2><p>The <strong>Elements</strong> panel now supports the <a href="https://web.dev/articles/at-property">@property CSS at-rule</a>. It lets you define <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Web/CSS/--*">CSS custom properties</a> explicitly and register them in a stylesheet without running any JavaScript.</p><p>To inspect your registered custom properties, in <strong>Elements</strong> &gt; <strong>Styles</strong>, hover over the property name and see its descriptors in a tooltip. In the tooltip, click the link to view the registered property in the collapsible <code>@property</code> section.</p><p><video class="screenshot" width="800" height="511" style="--vid-width: 800; --vid-height: 511" muted="" loop="" controls="" autoplay=""> <source src="https://storage.googleapis.com/web-dev-uploads/video/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/vDfXTULIyNIJXVw6lKvf.mp4" type="video/mp4"> </video></p><p>Chromium issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1471102">1471102</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1471103">1471103</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1471105">1471105</a>.</p><h2 id="overrides" tabindex="-1"><a href="#overrides" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> More local overrides improvements</h2><p>Continuing the stream of improvements in the <a href="/blog/new-in-devtools-117/#overrides">previous version</a>, <a href="/docs/devtools/overrides/">local overrides</a> now do the following:</p><ul><li><p>In <strong>Sources</strong> &gt; <strong>Page</strong>, when you right-click a source-mapped file and select <strong>Override content</strong>, DevTools will show a dialog that takes you to the original source instead. Contents of source-mapped files can't be overridden.</p><img width="800" height="458" src="https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/7pgnWI5CLcNBnv2H7aWT.png?auto=format" srcset="https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/7pgnWI5CLcNBnv2H7aWT.png?auto=format&amp;w=200 <strong>Experiments</strong>.</p><p>Chromium issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1472952">1472952</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1416338">1416338</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1472580">1472580</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1473681">1473681</a> <a href="https://crbug.com/1475668">1475668</a>.</p><h2 id="search" tabindex="-1"><a href="#search" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Enhanced search</h2><p><a href="/docs/devtools/search/"><strong>Search</strong></a> results now show an entry per all the matches it found in a line of code. Previously, it showed only the first match per line of code. The new behavior is especially useful when you search across minified files. When you click a search result, it opens the file in the editor and now scrolls the match into view not only vertically but also horizontally.</p><img width="800" height="424" src="https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/f5Yu4fSECIVDllWkpEZs.png?auto=format" sizes="(min-width:800px) 800px,calc(100vw - 48px)" alt="The before and after making search show all the matches per line." loading="lazy" decoding="async" srcset="https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/f5Yu4fSECIVDllWkpEZs.png?auto=format&amp;w=200 See the before (left) and after (right) comparison in the next video.</p><p><video class="screenshot" width="800" height="481" style="--vid-width: 800; --vid-height: 481" muted="" loop="" controls="" autoplay=""> <source src="https://storage.googleapis.com/web-dev-uploads/video/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/FyExrp5BLiGRHAT3OK4C.mp4" type="video/mp4"> </video></p><p>Finally, <strong>Search</strong> now supports <a href="/docs/devtools/settings/ignore-list/">ignore listing</a> and won't show you results from ignored files.</p><p>Chromium issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1468875">1468875</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1472019">1472019</a>.</p><h2 id="sources" tabindex="-1"><a href="#sources" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Improved Sources panel</h2><h3 id="workspace" tabindex="-1"><a href="#workspace" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Streamlined workspace in the Sources panel</h3><p>The <a href="/docs/devtools/workspaces/">workspace</a> feature in the <strong>Sources</strong> panel is new streamlined:</p><ul><li><strong>Consistent naming</strong>. Most notably, the <strong>Sources</strong> &gt; <strong>Filesystem</strong> pane was renamed into <strong>Workspace</strong>. Various UI texts in this pane are now clearer and free of redundancy.</li><li><strong>Improved setup</strong>. See better cues for dragging and dropping folders or click a link to select a folder.</li></ul><p><a href="/docs/devtools/workspaces/"><strong>Sources</strong> &gt; <strong>Workspace</strong></a> lets you sync changes you make in DevTools directly to your source files.</p><p>See the new setup and workflow in action:</p><p><video class="screenshot" width="800" height="436" style="--vid-width: 800; --vid-height: 436" muted="" loop="" controls="" autoplay=""> <source src="https://storage.googleapis.com/web-dev-uploads/video/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/1T78X6ldgLhiH6iJgAMk.mp4" type="video/mp4"> </video></p><p>Chromium issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1473771">1473771</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1473880">1473880</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1473963">1473963</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1474686">1474686</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1474687">1474687</a>.</p><h3 id="reorder-panes" tabindex="-1"><a href="#reorder-panes" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Reorder panes in Sources</h3><p>You can now reorder panes on the left side of the <strong>Sources</strong> panel by dragging and dropping, similar to how you can <a href="/docs/devtools/customize/#reorder">reorder other panels, tabs, and panes</a>.</p><p><video class="screenshot" width="800" height="375" style="--vid-width: 800; --vid-height: 375" muted="" issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1473758">1473758</a>.</p><h3 id="syntax" tabindex="-1"><a href="#syntax" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Syntax highlighting and pretty-printing for more script types</h3><p>The <strong>Sources</strong> panel can now:</p><ul><li>Pretty-print inline JavaScript within the following script types: <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Web/JavaScript/Guide/Modules"><code>module</code></a>, <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Web/HTML/Element/script/type/importmap"><code>importmap</code></a>, <a href="/blog/debugging-speculation-rules/"><code>speculationrules</code></a>.</li><li>Highlight the syntax of <code>importmap</code> and <code>speculationrules</code> script types, both of which hold JSON.</li></ul><img width="800" height="395" src="https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/yZYe1CF5ObuLu7zVjcot.png?auto=format" sizes="(min-width:800px) 800px,calc(100vw - 48px)" 1252w,https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/yZYe1CF5ObuLu7zVjcot.png?auto=format&amp;w=1428 1428w,https://wd.imgix.net/image/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/yZYe1CF5ObuLu7zVjcot.png?auto=format&amp;w=1600 1600w"><p>For more information on speculation rules, see <a href="/blog/prerender-pages/">Prerender pages in Chrome for instant page navigations</a>.</p><p>Chromium issue: <a href="https://crbug.com/1473875">1473875</a>.</p><h2 id="reduced-transparency" tabindex="-1"><a href="#reduced-transparency" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Emulate prefers-reduced-transparency media feature</h2><p><a href="/blog/chrome-118-beta/#media-queries-prefers-reduced-transparency-feature">Chrome 118 now supports</a> the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Web/CSS/@media/prefers-reduced-transparency"><code>prefers-reduced-transparency</code> media feature</a>. This feature lets developers adapt web content to user-selected preference for reduced transparency in the OS, such as the <strong>Reduce transparency</strong> setting on macOS.</p><p>To emulate this media feature, open the <strong>Rendering</strong> tab and scroll down to it.</p><p><video class="screenshot" width="800" height="533" style="--vid-width: 800; --vid-height: 533" muted="" loop="" controls="" autoplay=""> <source src="https://storage.googleapis.com/web-dev-uploads/video/NJdAV9UgKuN8AhoaPBquL7giZQo1/Xh60t9y0KnAIdwoUnbX5.mp4" type="video/mp4"> </video></p><p>Chromium issue: <a href="https://crbug.com/1424879">1424879</a>.</p><h2 id="lighthouse" tabindex="-1"><a href="#lighthouse" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Lighthouse 11</h2><p>The <strong>Lighthouse</strong> panel now runs <a href="/blog/lighthouse-11-0/">Lighthouse 11</a>. Most notably, this version removes legacy navigation and adds new accessibility audits and changes how the accessibility category is scored.</p><p>See also the <a href="https://github.com/GoogleChrome/lighthouse/releases/tag/v11.0.0">full list of changes</a>. To learn the basics of using the <strong>Lighthouse</strong> panel in DevTools, see <a href="/docs/devtools/lighthouse/">Lighthouse: Optimize website speed</a>.</p><p>Chromium issue: <a href="https://crbug.com/772558">772558</a>.</p><h2 id="accessibility" tabindex="-1"><a href="#accessibility" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Accessibility improvements</h2><p>DevTools now supports more navigation keystrokes:</p><ul><li><strong>CSS Overview</strong>: Use the up and down arrows to navigate sections in the left sidebar.</li><li><strong>Memory</strong>: In the left sidebar, focus the <strong>Save</strong> button next to snapshots with <kbd>Tab</kbd> and press <kbd>Enter</kbd> to select folder.</li></ul><p>Additionally, several screen reader announcement issues have been fixed.</p><p>Chromium issues: <a href="https://crbug.com/1470401">1470401</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1471301">1471301</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1474108">1474108</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1468631">1468631</a>.</p><h2 id="misc" tabindex="-1"><a href="#misc" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Miscellaneous highlights</h2><p>These are some noteworthy fixes and improvements in this release:</p><ul><li><strong>Network</strong>: New icons for popular resources types: <code>media</code>, <code>wasm</code>, <code>websocket</code>, <code>manifest</code>, <code>fetch/xhr</code>, <code>json</code> (<a href="https://crbug.com/1466298">1466298</a>).</li><li>Color updates to material 3 colors in many UI elements, most notably in the <strong>Elements</strong> and <strong>Performance</strong> panels (<a href="https://crbug.com/1456690">1456690</a>, <a href="https://crbug.com/1472243">1472243</a>).</li><li><strong>Issues</strong> now preserves cookie issues across navigations (<a href="https://crbug.com/1466601">1466601</a>).</li><li>Various <a href="/blog/new-in-devtools-117/#preloading"><strong>Application</strong> &gt; <strong>Preloading</strong></a> improvements, most notably sortable grids and revised rule set details (<a href="https://crbug.com/1410709">1410709</a>).</li><li>Various improvements of the command editor in <a href="/blog/new-in-devtools-117/#protocol-monitor"><strong>Protocol monitor</strong></a>, most notably warnings on wrong input, editing a sent command, editor for object parameters without predefined keys, support for enums undefined by references, objects without type reference, filter commands by substring matches, and more (<a href="https://crbug.com/1448050">1448050</a>).</li><li><strong>Performance</strong> flame chart gets a border around the total box on the pie chart (<a href="https://crbug.com/1470147">1470147</a>).</li><li><strong>Sources</strong> now doesn't treat dashes as word characters in CSS (<a href="https://crbug.com/1471354">1471354</a>).</li><li>Autocomplete now always sorts CSS-wise keywords at the end.</li><li>RegEx filters now support spaces (<a href="https://crbug.com/1346936">1346936</a>).</li><li><strong>Elements</strong> fixed media query feature detection (<a href="https://crbug.com/1472693">1472693</a>).</li></ul><h2 id="preview-channels" tabindex="-1"><a href="#preview-channels" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Download the preview channels</h2><p>Consider using the Chrome <a href="https://www.google.com/chrome/canary/">Canary</a>, <a href="https://www.google.com/chrome/dev/">Dev</a> or <a href="https://www.google.com/chrome/beta/">Beta</a> as your default development browser. These preview channels give you access to the latest DevTools features, test cutting-edge web platform APIs, and find issues on your site before your users do!</p><h2 id="contact-us" tabindex="-1"><a href="#contact-us" class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Getting in touch with the Chrome DevTools team</h2><p>Use the following options to discuss the new features and changes in the post, or anything else related to DevTools.</p><ul><li>Submit a suggestion or feedback to us via <a href="https://crbug.com">crbug.com</a>.</li><li>Report a DevTools issue using the <strong>More options</strong> &nbsp; <img width="4" height="20" src="https://wd.imgix.net/image/admin/4sdCQbpBaG4MpoHB1J08.png?auto=format" sizes="(min-width:4px) 4px,calc(100vw - 48px)" alt="More" loading="lazy"
